SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

2022-07-04 13:18:34.702 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (9ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

2022-07-04 20:47:59.147 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (5ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']

FROM "__EFMigrationsHistory"

2022-07-04 20:47:59.175 +00:00 [INF] No migrations were applied. The database is already up to date.
2022-07-04 20:47:59.233 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (11ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

2022-07-04 21:02:44.440 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (3ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )
